Datensatzgruppenabfrage                    : select account.a_code a_code ,decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,A_Name,Nvl(A_Name_Eng,A_Name)) A_name,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,Group_Name,Group_E_Name) Group_Name
 from account,account_grouping,account_curr
Where
account.a_grouping=account_grouping.group_no(+)
And account.a_code = account_curr.a_code
And account_curr.A_CY=:Parameter.Stk_Cur
and Exists  ( Select Account_Type  From Account_Types  Where Nvl (Affected_By_Trans, 0) = 1
And Account_Type = account.a_s_m) 
and Exists (select 1 from priv_acc where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and a_code=account.a_code 
And a_cy =account_curr.a_cy 
and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And account.a_code Like Decode(:ias_whtrns_mst.tr_a_code,Null,'%',:ias_whtrns_mst.tr_a_code||'%')
order by account.a_code

    And Nvl(inactive,0)  =0

                   Where request_types.out_trnsfr In (2,3) 
                    And ias_out_request_mst.out_req_type = request_types.req_type
                    And (request_types.Tr_Type Is Null Or request_types.Tr_Type =:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type)
 And RowNum <=1 
And Exists (Select 1 From priv_req_type
             Where priv_req_type.req_type = Request_types.req_type
             And Nvl(Fill_flag,0) = 1
             And RowNum <=1    ))
    And Nvl(inactive,0)  =0 
    And Nvl(approved,0)  =1 
And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,W_Code)
And Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0, Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code   ,0),1,F_W_Code) 
     = Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0,Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0) ,0,0,W_Code),1,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code)
And Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0),0,0,W_COde) = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0)
Order By out_req_type,
         out_req_no

       0 Avl_Qty,
0 I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1

            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
               And Rownum <= 1))
     And (   (Nvl(M.Service_Itm, 0) = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From Ias_Itm_Wcode

                   And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, W_Code)
                   And Nvl(Avl_Qty, 0) > 0
                   And Rownum <= 1))

                2, Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_F_Desc),

            Decode(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')

                2,Upper(I_Code || M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code),D.LVL_UNIT

   And  w_code =  Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Mst.F_w_code,:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.F_w_code)

   And  batch_no  Like Decode( :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no ,Null,'%', :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no||'%')

Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.P_Size,1)) > 0

    FROM IAS_RT_BILL_MST, S_FLAGS, IAS_RT_SALES_TYPES
   WHERE IAS_RT_BILL_MST.RT_BILL_DOC_TYPE = S_FLAGS.FLG_VALUE
     AND S_FLAGS.FLG_CODE = 'TYPE_NAME'
     AND S_FLAGS.LANG_NO = :PARAMETER.LANG_NO
     And Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_Code,0) = decode( Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_Code,0) ,0,0,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code)
     AND IAS_RT_BILL_MST.SR_TYPE = IAS_RT_SALES_TYPES.SR_TYPE
     AND 1 =
            (CASE
                WHEN :PARAMETER.USER_VIEW_DOC_ENTR = 0 THEN 1
                ELSE (SELECT 1
                        FROM IAS_SHW_DOC_PRIV
                       WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                         AND T_U_ID = IAS_RT_BILL_MST.AD_U_ID
                         AND NVL(PRIV_FLAG, 0) = 1
                         AND ROWNUM <= 1)
             END)
     AND (   (:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
          OR (EXISTS(
                 SELECT 1
                   FROM PRIVILEGE_WH
                  WHERE PRIVILEGE_WH.W_CODE = Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_CODE,PRIVILEGE_WH.W_CODE)
                    AND U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                    AND view_FLAG = 1
                    AND ROWNUM <= 1)))
     AND (   (:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
          OR EXISTS(
                SELECT 1
                  FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                 WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                   AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO = IAS_RT_BILL_MST.BRN_NO
                   AND NVL(VIEW_FLAG, 1) = 1
                   AND ROWNUM <= 1))
ORDER BY W_CODE, RT_BILL_DATE desc, RT_BILL_NO desc
